## [上海北外滩一游艇起火](https://m.weibo.cn/search?containerid=100103type%3D1%26t%3D10%26q%3D%23%E4%B8%8A%E6%B5%B7%E5%8C%97%E5%A4%96%E6%BB%A9%E4%B8%80%E6%B8%B8%E8%89%87%E8%B5%B7%E7%81%AB%23&isnewpage=1&extparam=seat%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot%26dgr%3D0%26cate%3D0%26pos%3D49%26realpos%3D49%26flag%3D0%26c_type%3D31%26display_time%3D1628352119%26pre_seqid%3D1628352119312021266227&luicode=10000011&lfid=106003type%3D25%26t%3D3%26disable_hot%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot) `社会` 
 8月7日晚7时19分，上海北外滩地区白玉兰码头附近江面一艘游艇着火，现场有明火。据上海消防通报，火势已经被控制，据相关部门信息反馈，没有人员被困。
## [邓亚萍谈樊振东奥运表现](https://m.weibo.cn/search?containerid=100103type%3D1%26t%3D10%26q%3D%23%E9%82%93%E4%BA%9A%E8%90%8D%E8%B0%88%E6%A8%8A%E6%8C%AF%E4%B8%9C%E5%A5%A5%E8%BF%90%E8%A1%A8%E7%8E%B0%23&isnewpage=1&extparam=seat%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot%26dgr%3D0%26cate%3D0%26pos%3D50%26realpos%3D50%26flag%3D0%26c_type%3D31%26display_time%3D1628352119%26pre_seqid%3D1628352119312021266227&luicode=10000011&lfid=106003type%3D25%26t%3D3%26disable_hot%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot) `体育` 
 邓亚萍复盘樊振东男团决赛表现，在理性分析樊振东的问题时也肯定了樊振东的表现，并称樊振东与奥恰洛夫的对战值得反复回看、总结和反思。
